# LineProof Mega Design Transformation — VAR Edition

5000 tasks. Dual-surface: B2B cockpit untouched, Arena carries the football broadcast layer. Regenerate with `node scripts/gen-design-checklist.js`.

## D1 — VAR concept lock (ship day 1)

- [ ] 0001 Adopt the VAR metaphor: agent as autonomous video-assistant referee for markets
- [ ] 0002 Map verdicts to referee language: CLEAN = play on, WATCH = yellow card, FLAGGED = red card
- [ ] 0003 Ship /arena Match Center consuming the existing APIs only — zero backend risk
- [ ] 0004 Link Arena from the main nav without disturbing the B2B cockpit
- [ ] 0005 Deploy and verify the Arena renders from live feed data

## D2 — Stadium visual system

- [ ] 0006 Pitch-green dark palette layered over the existing brand tokens
- [ ] 0007 Scoreboard numeral style for scores and clocks
- [ ] 0008 Broadcast lower-third component for fixture identity
- [ ] 0009 Floodlight radial lighting on section headers
- [ ] 0010 Card-flash animation for yellow and red verdicts

## D3 — Match HUD

- [ ] 0011 Live minute clock derived from feed score updates
- [ ] 0012 Fair-line versus quoted-line bar duel per outcome
- [ ] 0013 Margin meter styled as possession bar
- [ ] 0014 Verdict card raised with referee-arm timing curve

## D4 — Whistle moments

- [ ] 0015 Anomaly timeline rendered as match incidents feed
- [ ] 0016 Incident chips: minute, fixture, offence code, severity card
- [ ] 0017 Replay scrubber over archived scans

## D5 — On-chain tunnel

- [ ] 0018 Attestation trail as post-match referee report
- [ ] 0019 Signature rows styled as official match documents
- [ ] 0020 Verification MATCH state as full-time whistle moment

## D6 — Motion pass

- [ ] 0021 Entrance choreography: staggered lower-thirds, no dead frames
- [ ] 0022 Idle drift on resting panels to keep broadcast liveliness
- [ ] 0023 Reduced-motion fallback for accessibility

## D7 — Copy pass (human, natural)

- [ ] 0024 Rewrite every Arena string in match-commentary register
- [ ] 0025 Zero emoji, zero stock AI phrasing, paraphrase everything
- [ ] 0026 Terminology sheet: offence codes, card language, referee report

## D8 — Responsive + performance

- [ ] 0027 Arena readable on mobile: single-column HUD
- [ ] 0028 No layout shift on data refresh
- [ ] 0029 Lighthouse pass over 90 performance on the Arena

## D9 — Demo integration

- [ ] 0030 Capture Arena frames headlessly for the video walkthrough
- [ ] 0031 Insert Arena scene into the Remotion sequence
- [ ] 0032 Re-render final MP4 and refresh the Download package

## D10 — Judge polish

- [ ] 0033 Cross-check every judging criterion against the Arena surface
- [ ] 0034 Dry-run the 30-second judge path through both surfaces
- [ ] 0035 Freeze design two days before the deadline

## D11-D14 — Post-deadline GameFi track (startup lane)

- [ ] 0036 Design prediction-league concept on top of integrity scores
- [ ] 0037 Fan-facing card-collection concept for verified match incidents
- [ ] 0038 Season pass concept tied to attestation history
- [ ] 0039 Scope on-chain settlement design for the league
